{"code":1,"isDone":false,"toInsertArticleList":[{"createdTime":"2020-09-16 13:03:27","updatedTime":"2020-09-16 13:03:27","title":"The Gravity Cube Click Clock Eliminates Fumbling in the Dark","link":"https://design-milk.com/?p=428651","description":"<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/the-gravity-cube-click-clock-eliminates-fumbling-in-the-dark/gingko-gravity-cube-click-clock-1/\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Gingko-Gravity-Cube-Click-Clock-1-810x446.jpg\" alt=\"The Gravity Cube Click Clock Eliminates Fumbling in the Dark\" /></a></p> \n<p>UK-based <a href=\"https://shop.design-milk.com/collections/gingko\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" data-wpel-link=\"exclude\">Gingko</a>, which was founded in 2011 by husband-and-wife duo Paul and Natalie Sun, brings their love of innovative electronics to their collection of well-made, functional products that are fun to use and show off. One of our favorites, the <a href=\"https://shop.design-milk.com/collections/gingko/products/gravity-cube-click-clock\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" data-wpel-link=\"exclude\">Gravity Cube Click Clock</a>, is a minimalist alarm clock that makes getting up in the morning not so bad. If you want to snooze, just touch the top of the cube and if you’re ready to turn the alarm off, just turn the clock over onto any side. Both scenarios mean you won’t be fumbling in the dark trying to find the snooze or off button when you’re still half asleep. At a compact 3″ x 3″ x 3″ size, the clock takes up little real estate on your bedside table and its sleek rubberized finish makes it soft to the touch.</p> \n<p><a href=\"https://shop.design-milk.com/collections/gingko/products/gravity-cube-click-clock\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-428653 noopener noreferrer\" data-wpel-link=\"exclude\"><img class=\"alignnone wp-image-428653 size-large\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Gingko-Gravity-Cube-Click-Clock-1m-810x705.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"705\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Gingko-Gravity-Cube-Click-Clock-1m-810x705.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Gingko-Gravity-Cube-Click-Clock-1m-800x696.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Gingko-Gravity-Cube-Click-Clock-1m-768x668.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Gingko-Gravity-Cube-Click-Clock-1m-500x435.jpg 500w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Gingko-Gravity-Cube-Click-Clock-1m.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p> \n<p>The Gravity Cube Click Clock is outfitted with sound activated LED display technology which means it will alternate through the time, date, and temperature simply by snapping your fingers or clapping your hands. You can also set the display to just show the time instead of alternating through. During the night if you want to check the time, gently tap your bedside table or snap your fingers and the time will pop up for you. The clock also automatically dims between the hours of 9pm and 7am.</p> \n<p><a href=\"https://shop.design-milk.com/collections/gingko/products/gravity-cube-click-clock\" rel=\"attachment g":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx27/cdn53@2020_3/2020/09/16/05-03-59-493_44b069e8e087257a.webp","https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Gingko-Gravity-Cube-Click-Clock-7.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx11/cdn95@2020_6/2020/09/16/05-03-44-040_885ea695b1bbe3e8.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~r/design-milk/~4/M5o37WOXJN8":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx22/cdn63@2020_3/2020/09/16/05-03-43-046_0c683c6cbc56b933.webp"},"publishedOrCreatedDate":1600232607173},{"createdTime":"2020-09-16 13:03:27","updatedTime":"2020-09-16 13:03:27","title":"Revitalizing Biodiversity with 3D-Printed Coral Tiles","link":"https://design-milk.com/?p=424827","description":"<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/revitalizing-biodiversity-with-3d-printed-coral-tiles/hku-3dprinted-tiles-3/\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/08/HKU-3Dprinted-tiles-3-810x540.jpg\" alt=\"Revitalizing Biodiversity with 3D-Printed Coral Tiles\" /></a></p> \n<p>Following the 3D-printed footsteps of <a href=\"https://design-milk.com/volvo-living-seawall-tiles/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\">previous efforts</a> to save coastal marine biodiversity utilizing technology and biomimicry, architects and marine scientists at the <a href=\"https://aal.hku.hk/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer external\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">University of Hong Kong (HKU)</a> have jointly developed a novel method for coral restoration making use of specially designed 3D-printed artificial ‘reef tiles’ for attachment by corals to enhance their chance of survival in the Hoi Ha Wan Marine Park in Hong Kong waters.</p> \n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=424829\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-424829\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-424829\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/08/HKU-3Dprinted-tiles-5-810x540.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"540\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/08/HKU-3Dprinted-tiles-5-810x540.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/08/HKU-3Dprinted-tiles-5-800x533.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/08/HKU-3Dprinted-tiles-5-768x512.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/08/HKU-3Dprinted-tiles-5-500x333.jpg 500w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/08/HKU-3Dprinted-tiles-5.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p> \n<p>A project commissioned by the Agriculture, Fisheries and Conservation Department (AFCD) to combat bio-erosion of essential coral habitat home to more than 120 fish species, architects from HKU’s Robotic Fabrication Lab, under the Fabrication and Material Technologies Lab of the Faculty of Architecture, and marine scientists from the Swire Institute of Marine Science (SWIMS) of the Faculty of Science at HKU collaborated to develop reef tiles printed with intricate detailing optimized to invite live coral attachment.</p> \n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=424830\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-424830\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-424830\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/08/HKU-3Dprinted-tiles-7-810x456.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"456\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/08/HKU-3Dprinted-tiles-7-810x456.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/08/HKU-3Dprinted-tiles-7-800x450.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/08/HKU-3Dprinted-tiles-7-768x432.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/08/HKU-3Dprinted-tiles-7-500x281.jpg 500w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/08/HKU-3Dprinted-tiles-7.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p> \n<p>The reef tiles were 3D-printed using reef-safe terracotta, using a robotic 3D clay printing method before firing each piece at 1,125 degrees Celsius to eventually be seeded with coral fragments. The finished pieces were then introduced within three selected sites across the Hoi Ha Wan Marine Park in Hong Kong waters.</p> \n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=424831\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-424831\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-424831\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/08/HKU-3Dprinted-tiles-2-810x619.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"619\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/08/HKU-3Dprinted-tiles-2-810x619.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/08/HKU-3Dprinted-tiles-2-800x611.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/08/HKU-3Dprinted-tiles-2-768x587.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/08/HKU-3Dprinted-tiles-2-500x382.jpg 500w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/08/HKU-3Dprinted-tiles-2.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p> \n<p>Though beautiful in their own right, the intricate patterns of each tile aren’t merely aesthetic, but designed to represent different growth forms of branching patterns of three endemic coral species – staghorn, massive brain and foliose plating colony forms – and optimize restoration of the ailing coral communities.</p> \n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=424832\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-424832\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-424832\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/08/HKU-3Dprinted-tiles-4.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"780\" height=\"470\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/08/HKU-3Dprinted-tiles-4.jpg 780w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/08/HKU-3Dprinted-tiles-4-768x463.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/08/HKU-3Dprinted-tiles-4-500x301.jpg 500w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 780px) 100vw, 780px\" /></a></p> \n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=424833\" square meters in total. Winners will be announced on April 15, 2021 and we’ll be sure to share our favorites here.</p> \n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=428765\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-428765\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-428765\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/a-design-award-cloud-art-poster-big-810x1002.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"1002\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/a-design-award-cloud-art-poster-big-810x1002.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/a-design-award-cloud-art-poster-big-800x990.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/a-design-award-cloud-art-poster-big-768x950.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/a-design-award-cloud-art-poster-big-1241x1536.jpg 1241w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/a-design-award-cloud-art-poster-big-500x619.jpg 500w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/a-design-award-cloud-art-poster-big.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p> \n<p>This is an award that has immense benefits. 13:03:27","updatedTime":"2020-09-16 13:03:27","title":"La Visione: A Restaurant with a Fresh, Colorful Design Featuring Carpet Collages","link":"https://design-milk.com/?p=428674","description":"<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/la-visione-a-restaurant-with-a-fresh-colorful-design-featuring-carpet-collages/object-carpet-restaurant-lavisione-ippolito-fleitz-1/\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Object-Carpet-Restaurant-LaVisione-Ippolito-Fleitz-1-810x608.jpg\" alt=\"La Visione: A Restaurant with a Fresh, Colorful Design Featuring Carpet Collages\" /></a></p> \n<p>At carpet supplier Object Carpet’s headquarters, ‘Object Campus – City of Visions,’ <a href=\"https://ifgroup.org/en/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer external\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">Ippolito Fleitz Group</a> designed the interior and branding for their restaurant <a href=\"https://ifgroup.org/en/project/13317/la-visione/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer external\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">La Visione</a>. In addition to serving everyone food, the Italian restaurant serves as a co-working space, meeting spot and bar, accomplishing their desire to build a central location for networking and to create “vital cross-industry synergies.” The Denkendorf, Germany based company’s new restaurant is separated into three areas – a lounge, dining area and a vinoteca – all of which transition as needed for different functions throughout the day.</p> \n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/la-visione-a-restaurant-with-a-fresh-colorful-design-featuring-carpet-collages/object-carpet-restaurant-lavisione-ippolito-fleitz-1m/\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-428677\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-428677\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Object-Carpet-Restaurant-LaVisione-Ippolito-Fleitz-1m-810x1080.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"1080\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Object-Carpet-Restaurant-LaVisione-Ippolito-Fleitz-1m-810x1080.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Object-Carpet-Restaurant-LaVisione-Ippolito-Fleitz-1m-800x1067.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Object-Carpet-Restaurant-LaVisione-Ippolito-Fleitz-1m-768x1024.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Object-Carpet-Restaurant-LaVisione-Ippolito-Fleitz-1m-1152x1536.jpg 1152w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Object-Carpet-Restaurant-LaVisione-Ippolito-Fleitz-1m-500x667.jpg 500w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Object-Carpet-Restaurant-LaVisione-Ippolito-Fleitz-1m.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p> \n<p>The dining area brings together an adventurous experience of aromas, sounds and tastes, visually experienced through a fresh palette of colors and fabrics. The space is decorated with textile wall collages using the brand’s damask and burlap fabrics alongside carpet and cord as a tangible display of their expertise.</p> \n<p><a 09-16 13:03:27","updatedTime":"2020-09-16 13:03:27","title":"Ukurant Puts Young Danish Designers Front + Center","link":"https://design-milk.com/?p=428510","description":"<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/ukurant-puts-young-danish-designers-front-center/ukurant-featured-image/\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Ukurant-Featured-Image-810x540.jpg\" alt=\"Ukurant Puts Young Danish Designers Front + Center\" /></a></p> \n<p>Denmark’s annual <a href=\"https://3daysofdesign.dk/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer external\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">3 Days of Design</a> event occurred earlier this month, with one of the creative exhibits – <a href=\"https://ukurant.com/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer external\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">Ukurant</a> – presenting works by select young Danish designers in Ukurant Objects. The overall focus was on how a new generation challenges traditions through experimenting with materials and technologies and revising aesthetics and commercial design. <a href=\"https://shop.design-milk.com/collections/furniture\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" data-wpel-link=\"exclude\">Furniture</a>, textiles, ceramics, lighting and more put their fresh perspectives front and center. Each piece challenges the idea of sculptural objects versus functional.</p> \n<div> \n <div id=\"attachment_428525\" class=\"wp-caption alignnone\">\n  <a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=428525\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-428525\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"size-large wp-image-428525\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Ukurant-Alexander-Kirkeby-810x1215.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"1215\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Ukurant-Alexander-Kirkeby-810x1215.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Ukurant-Alexander-Kirkeby-800x1200.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Ukurant-Alexander-Kirkeby-768x1152.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Ukurant-Alexander-Kirkeby-1024x1536.jpg 1024w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Ukurant-Alexander-Kirkeby-500x750.jpg 500w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Ukurant-Alexander-Kirkeby.jpg 1333w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a>\n  <p class=\"wp-caption-text\">Alexander Kirkeby</p>\n </div> \n <p>Ukurant itself is a curated platform showcasing experimental design objects created by 24 talented young designers. Put together by Josefine Krabbe Munck, Kamma Rosa Schytte, Kasper Kyster and Lærke Ryom, the foursome founded Ukurant as a professional community for graduates to share experiences, networks, project ideas and collaborations.</p> \n <div id=\"attachment_428548\" class=\"wp-caption alignnone\">\n  <a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=428548\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-428548\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"size-full wp-image-428548\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Ukurant-group-photo.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"540\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Ukurant-group-photo.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Ukurant-group-photo-800x533.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Ukurant-group-photo-768x512.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Ukurant-group-photo-500x333.jpg 500w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a>\n  <p class=\"wp-caption-text\">Ukurant’s Founders</p>\n </div> \n <div id=\"attachment_428526\" class=\"wp-caption alignnone\">\n  <a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=428526\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-428526\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"size-full wp-image-428526\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Ukurant-Anders-Nyberg.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"1215\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Ukurant-Anders-Nyberg.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Ukurant-Anders-Nyberg-800x1200.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Ukurant-Anders-Nyberg-768x1152.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Ukurant-Anders-Nyberg-500x750.jpg 500w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a>\n  <p class=\"wp-caption-text\">Anders Olof Nyberg</p>\n </div> \n <p>The designers on display in Ukurant Objects include Alexander Kirkeby, Anders Olof Nyberg, Anna Søgaard, Bjarke Ballisager, Bonnie Hvillum, Christian &amp; Jade, Davide Ronco, Esben Kaldahl, Felicia Arvid, Ida Elke, Kamma Rosa Schytte, Kasper Kyster, Lærke Ryom, Margarida L. Pereira, OTTOTTO, Sia Hurtigkarl Degel, Pia Angela Rasmussen, Simone Øster, Josefine Krabbe Munck, Sisse Holst Pedersen, Therese Hald Boesen and Tronhjem Rømer.</p> \n <div id=\"attachment_428527\" shedOrCreatedDate":1600232607164},{"createdTime":"2020-09-16 13:03:27","updatedTime":"2020-09-16 13:03:27","title":"Studio Nienke Hoogvliet Turns Seaweed and Fish Skin into Rugs, Fabrics + Leather","link":"https://design-milk.com/?p=428329","description":"<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/studio-nienke-hoogvliet-turns-seaweed-and-fish-skin-into-rugs-fabrics-leather/design_milk_circular_by_design_re_sea_me_02/\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Design_Milk_Circular_by_Design_Re_Sea_Me_02-810x540.jpg\" alt=\"Studio Nienke Hoogvliet Turns Seaweed and Fish Skin into Rugs, Fabrics + Leather\" /></a></p> \n<p>Based in The Hague, in The Netherlands, <a href=\"https://www.nienkehoogvliet.nl/\" data-wpel-link=\"external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"external noopener noreferrer\">Studio Nienke Hoogvliet</a> is a design studio specializing in material research, experimental and conceptual design. Nienke Hoogvliet founded the studio in 2013, and has since been joined by Tim Jongerius. The pair now engage in freelance projects as well as self-initiated research and design projects that raise awareness of social and environmental problems in the textile, leather and food industry. By creating innovative material alternatives, they hope to change both perspectives and systems.</p> \n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/studio-nienke-hoogvliet-turns-seaweed-and-fish-skin-into-rugs-fabrics-leather/design_milk_circular_by_design_resea_me_nienke_tim_01/\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-428335\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-428335\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Design_Milk_Circular_by_Design_ReSea_Me_Nienke_Tim_01-810x607.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"607\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Design_Milk_Circular_by_Design_ReSea_Me_Nienke_Tim_01-810x607.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Design_Milk_Circular_by_Design_ReSea_Me_Nienke_Tim_01-800x600.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Design_Milk_Circular_by_Design_ReSea_Me_Nienke_Tim_01-768x576.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Design_Milk_Circular_by_Design_ReSea_Me_Nienke_Tim_01-500x375.jpg 500w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Design_Milk_Circular_by_Design_ReSea_Me_Nienke_Tim_01.jpg 1273w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p> \n<p><strong>Tell me a little bit about your childhood, education and background in terms of how you first became interested in creativity, design and sustainability.</strong></p> \n<p>Nienke: I grew up in The Hague, a city near the beach in the Netherlands. This is where my love for the beach and the sea started. My mom was always making things: sewing my clothes, building new closets or painting something a new color. I inherited her love of textiles and making. At a young age, she taught me how to use the sewing machine and my creativity could then flow freely. I was a very idealistic child. I raised petitions against animal testing, didn’t want to eat meat from the age of seven… Later, I went to the Willem de Kooning Academy – an art school in Rotterdam – and there I learned more about concept development, research and design. I also realized that art or design can be a way to raise awareness and to tell stories. After just three months, I decided that I wanted to have my own design studio and show the world how, with my designs, I could change it for the better. I started Studio Nienke Hoogvliet immediately after graduating in 2013,</p> \n<p>Tim: I also grew up in The Hague. As a child, I was already fascinated by how things work. When I was driving with my parents along the highway I could remember every building project there and could explain the progress they had made since the last time we passed it. This way of looking at things developed into questioning things: “Why are things the way they are?” and “Can’t we do better?” At the faculty of Architecture of TU Delft, I developed my ‘research and design for a better world’ mentality further, gaining my Master’s in 2017. Nienke and I met each other in 2005 (at high school!) and since that time we have grown together and embraced the idea that design is the way to change perspectives.</p> \n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/studio-nienke-hoogvliet-turns-seaweed-and-fish-skin-into-rugs-fabrics-leather/design_milk_circular_by_design_sea_me_01/\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-428336\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-428336\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Design_Milk_Circular_by_Design_Sea_Me_01-810x540.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"540\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Design_Milk_Circular_by_Design_Sea_Me_01-810x540.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Design_Milk_Circular_by_Design_Sea_Me_01-800x533.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Design_Milk_Circular_by_Design_Sea_Me_01-768x512.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Design_Milk_Circular_by_Design_Sea_Me_01-500x333.jpg 500w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Design_Milk_Circular_by_Design_Sea_Me_01.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p> \n<p><strong>How would you describe your SEA ME and RE-SEA ME projects?</strong></p> \n<p>SEA ME is an ongoing research project into how seaweed could be used as a sustainable alternative for textiles and dyes. The SEA ME rug is made of seaweed yarn, knotted by hand into a discarded fishing net to show the duality of the pollution of the ocean and all the beauty and solutions it could offer. Seaweed is a wonderful material, it doesn’t need freshwater or pesticides or insecticides to grow and it doesn’t take up agricultural land.</p> \n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/studio-nienke-hoogvliet-turns-seaweed-and-fish-skin-into-rugs-fabrics-leather/design_milk_circular_by_design_re_sea_me_04/\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-428333\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-428333\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Design_Milk_Circular_by_Design_Re_Sea_Me_04-810x810.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"810\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Design_Milk_Circular_by_Design_Re_Sea_Me_04-810x810.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Design_Milk_Circular_by_Design_Re_Sea_Me_04-800x800.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Design_Milk_Circular_by_Design_Re_Sea_Me_04-100x100.jpg 100w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Design_Milk_Circular_by_Design_Re_Sea_Me_04-768x768.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Design_Milk_Circular_by_Design_Re_Sea_Me_04-300x300.jpg 300w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Design_Milk_Circular_by_Design_Re_Sea_Me_04-500x500.jpg 500w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Design_Milk_Circular_by_Design_Re_Sea_Me_04.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p> \n<p>RE-SEA ME is another research project into which sustainable materials can be created from the ocean. Fish skin is often wasted by the fishing industry, and it can be turned into beautiful leather. This project wants to raise awareness for the same topic as SEA ME, but it shows another potentially sustainable material from the sea. We made a rug, hand-sewn in a discarded fishing net to show the continuation of the topic. And a stool, to show how strong the fish leather is. It’s one of the amazing qualities that fish leather is actually stronger than ‘regular’ leather since fish have a different type of connective tissue.</p> \n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/studio-nienke-hoogvliet-turns-seaweed-and-fish-skin-into-rugs-fabrics-leather/design_milk_circular_by_design_sea_me_04/\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-428339\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-428339\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Design_Milk_Circular_by_Design_Sea_Me_04-810x540.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"540\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Design_Milk_Circular_by_Design_Sea_Me_04-810x540.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Design_Milk_Circular_by_Design_Sea_Me_04-800x533.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Design_Milk_Circular_by_Design_Sea_Me_04-768x512.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Design_Milk_Circular_by_Design_Sea_Me_04-500x333.jpg 500w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Design_Milk_Circular_by_Design_Sea_Me_04.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p> \n<p><strong>What inspired this project?</strong></p> \n<p>Nienke’s love for nature and the oceans. The urgency to treat them differently, to stop polluting and to see their beauty and potential.</p> \n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/studio-nienke-hoogvliet-turns-seaweed-and-fish-skin-into-rugs-fabrics-leather/design_milk_circular_by_design_sea_me_11/\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-428352\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-428352\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Design_Milk_Circular_by_Design_Sea_Me_11-810x454.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"454\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Design_Milk_Circular_by_Design_Sea_Me_11-810x454.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Design_Milk_Circular_by_Design_Sea_Me_11-800x449.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Design_Milk_Circular_by_Design_Sea_Me_11-768x431.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Design_Milk_Circular_by_Design_Sea_Me_11-500x281.jpg 500w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Design_Milk_Circular_by_Design_Sea_Me_11.jpg 1278w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p> \n<p><strong>What waste (and other) materials are you using, how did you select those particular materials and how do you source them?</strong></p> \n<p>As well as seaweed and fish skins, we have also collaborated with the Dutch Water Authorities, to work with materials reclaimed or created from wastewater. These include reclaimed toilet paper and bio-plastic made from the bacteria that clean the wastewater. Those collaborations were super interesting and we never expected that even wastewater could be such an interesting source of raw materials. It’s very important to show, that even such strange – and let’s be honest dirty, materials can have so much value. If people realized and accepted this, the change to recycling more materials would be easier to make.</p> \n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/studio-nienke-hoogvliet-turns-seaweed-and-fish-skin-into-rugs-fabrics-leather/design_milk_circular_by_design_sea_me_09/\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-428344\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-428344\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Design_Milk_Circular_by_Design_Sea_Me_09-810x478.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"478\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Design_Milk_Circular_by_Design_Sea_Me_09-810x478.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Design_Milk_Circular_by_Design_Sea_Me_09-800x472.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Design_Milk_Circular_by_Design_Sea_Me_09-768x453.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Design_Milk_Circular_by_Design_Sea_Me_09-500x295.jpg 500w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Design_Milk_Circular_by_Design_Sea_Me_09.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p> \n<p><strong>When did you first become interested in using waste as raw material and what motivated this decision?</strong></p> \n<p>It was never our goal to use waste – we work from a holistic point of view, which means that we try to take all aspects around a production process into consideration. That often leads to the realization that somewhere in the process, valuable material is not being used. To close that circle, it makes sense to use that material.</p> \n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/studio-nienke-hoogvliet-turns-seaweed-and-fish-skin-into-rugs-fabrics-leather/design_milk_circular_by_design_sea_me_07/\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-428342\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-428342\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Design_Milk_Circular_by_Design_Sea_Me_07-810x810.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"810\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Design_Milk_Circular_by_Design_Sea_Me_07-810x810.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Design_Milk_Circular_by_Design_Sea_Me_07-800x800.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Design_Milk_Circular_by_Design_Sea_Me_07-100x100.jpg 100w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Design_Milk_Circular_by_Design_Sea_Me_07-768x768.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Design_Milk_Circular_by_Design_Sea_Me_07-300x300.jpg 300w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Design_Milk_Circular_by_Design_Sea_Me_07-500x500.jpg 500w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Design_Milk_Circular_by_Design_Sea_Me_07.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p> \n<p><strong>What processes do the materials have to undergo to become the finished product?</strong></p> \n<p>The fish skin is turned into leather through natural tanning. We wrote a book, <em>Fish Leather</em>, to explain the process, so everyone can learn how to do it and it’s actually very easy – it just requires oils and lots of manual labor. For the seaweed it’s more complicated, it requires machines and cannot be done by hand. But the waste from one process can be used for another application, as we showed in the SEA ME Collection. The seating of the chair is made from seaweed yarn, the ‘waste’ of that process is made into a textile dye and is used to dye the seating, the leftovers of the dyeing process are used to create a regular paint for the tabletop, and a bioplastic like material. We fully use the seaweed and have no waste left.</p> \n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/studio-nienke-hoogvliet-turns-seaweed-and-fish-skin-into-rugs-fabrics-leather/design_milk_circular_by_design_sea_me_05/\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-428340\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-428340\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Design_Milk_Circular_by_Design_Sea_Me_05-810x540.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"540\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Design_Milk_Circular_by_Design_Sea_Me_05-810x540.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Design_Milk_Circular_by_Design_Sea_Me_05-800x533.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Design_Milk_Circular_by_Design_Sea_Me_05-768x512.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Design_Milk_Circular_by_Design_Sea_Me_05-500x333.jpg 500w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Design_Milk_Circular_by_Design_Sea_Me_05.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p> \n<p><strong>What happens to your products at the end of their life – can they go back into the circular economy?</strong></p> \n<p>When they cannot be re-used or recycled anymore, they can be composted and this way they can become food for the soil again. All the materials are biodegradable.</p> \n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/studio-nienke-hoogvliet-turns-seaweed-and-fish-skin-into-rugs-fabrics-leather/design_milk_circular_by_design_re_sea_me_01/\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-428330\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-428330\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Design_Milk_Circular_by_Design_Re_Sea_Me_01-810x540.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"540\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Design_Milk_Circular_by_Design_Re_Sea_Me_01-810x540.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Design_Milk_Circular_by_Design_Re_Sea_Me_01-800x533.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Design_Milk_Circular_by_Design_Re_Sea_Me_01-768x512.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Design_Milk_Circular_by_Design_Re_Sea_Me_01-500x333.jpg 500w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Design_Milk_Circular_by_Design_Re_Sea_Me_01.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p> \n<p><strong>How did you feel the first time you saw the transformation from waste material to product/prototype?</strong></p> \n<p>When you are doing research and experimenting, the change from waste material to product happens slowly and gradually. At first, you are only paying attention to all the things that don’t work. When you are mastering a material more and more, you start to see the potential and that’s when you get excited. Sometimes it can still feel strange, for example, Nienke is scared of fish and during the tanning sometimes she still feels a bit disgusted, but when the end product is complete, it feels great to have given value back to something, so it’s all worth it in the end.</p> \n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/studio-nienke-hoogvliet-turns-seaweed-and-fish-skin-into-rugs-fabrics-leather/design_milk_circular_by_design_re_sea_me_05/\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-428334\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-428334\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Design_Milk_Circular_by_Design_Re_Sea_Me_05-810x540.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"540\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Design_Milk_Circular_by_Design_Re_Sea_Me_05-810x540.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Design_Milk_Circular_by_Design_Re_Sea_Me_05-800x534.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Design_Milk_Circular_by_Design_Re_Sea_Me_05-768x512.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Design_Milk_Circular_by_Design_Re_Sea_Me_05-500x334.jpg 500w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Design_Milk_Circular_by_Design_Re_Sea_Me_05.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p> \n<p><strong>How have people reacted to this project?</strong></p> \n<p>We received so many positive responses! Everyone always wonders if the products smell (they don’t!) and they are amazed by the qualities and properties of the materials. We think we have changed a lot of perspectives and are looking forward to continuing to do that with all our projects.</p> \n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/studio-nienke-hoogvliet-turns-seaweed-and-fish-skin-into-rugs-fabrics-leather/design_milk_circular_by_design_re_sea_me_03/\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-428332\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-428332\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Design_Milk_Circular_by_Design_Re_Sea_Me_03-810x540.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"540\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Design_Milk_Circular_by_Design_Re_Sea_Me_03-810x540.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Design_Milk_Circular_by_Design_Re_Sea_Me_03-800x533.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Design_Milk_Circular_by_Design_Re_Sea_Me_03-768x512.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Design_Milk_Circular_by_Design_Re_Sea_Me_03-500x333.jpg 500w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Design_Milk_Circular_by_Design_Re_Sea_Me_03.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p> \n<p><strong>How do you feel opinions towards waste as a raw material are changing?</strong></p> \n<p>They are changing for sure. More and more people realize that we cannot maintain this linear economy and that we have to look into the possibilities of waste as a material. But even more important, more people understand that – and why – we should move towards a circular economy. It is not just about reusing waste, it’s about looking at processes with the aim to not exhaust the planet, the people or the animals. Reusing waste is one of the solutions, but we need to think further, deeper and in circles. We can see that awareness is starting to arise.</p> \n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/studio-nienke-hoogvliet-turns-seaweed-and-fish-skin-into-rugs-fabrics-leather/design_milk_circular_by_design_sea_me_06/\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-428341\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-428341\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Design_Milk_Circular_by_Design_Sea_Me_06-810x810.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"810\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Design_Milk_Circular_by_Design_Sea_Me_06-810x810.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Design_Milk_Circular_by_Design_Sea_Me_06-800x800.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Design_Milk_Circular_by_Design_Sea_Me_06-100x100.jpg 100w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Design_Milk_Circular_by_Design_Sea_Me_06-768x768.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Design_Milk_Circular_by_Design_Sea_Me_06-300x300.jpg 300w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Design_Milk_Circular_by_Design_Sea_Me_06-500x500.jpg 500w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Design_Milk_Circular_by_Design_Sea_Me_06.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p> \n<p><strong>What do you think the future holds for waste as a raw material?</strong></p> \n<p>We hope that it will become normal to use waste as a raw material and that there will be no more waste – just more resources.</p> \n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/studio-nienke-hoogvliet-turns-seaweed-and-fish-skin-into-rugs-fabrics-leather/design_milk_circular_by_design_sea_me_10/\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-428345\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-428345\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Design_Milk_Circular_by_Design_Sea_Me_10-810x506.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"506\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Design_Milk_Circular_by_Design_Sea_Me_10-810x506.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Design_Milk_Circular_by_Design_Sea_Me_10-800x500.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Design_Milk_Circular_by_Design_Sea_Me_10-768x480.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Design_Milk_Circular_by_Design_Sea_Me_10-500x313.jpg 500w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Design_Milk_Circular_by_Design_Sea_Me_10.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p> \n<p>Product photos by Femke Poort.<br /> Process photos by Hannah Braeken.</p> \n<p><a href=\"https://katietreggiden.com/designmilk/\" ","https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Design_Milk_Circular_by_Design_Re_Sea_Me_05-810x540.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx7/cdn56@2020_5/2020/09/16/05-03-50-668_07d8fb4fbd8ea01f.webp","https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Design_Milk_Circular_by_Design_Re_Sea_Me_03-810x540.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx30/cdn92@2020_1/2020/09/16/05-03-45-778_9d162135281f499c.webp","https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Design_Milk_Circular_by_Design_Sea_Me_06-810x810.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx1/cdn55@2020_4/2020/09/16/05-03-43-087_3d160ad5dca8cdb2.webp","https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Design_Milk_Circular_by_Design_Sea_Me_10-810x506.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx4/cdn87@2020_6/2020/09/16/05-03-49-227_1dbc3ba3b29a4392.webp","https://katietreggiden.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Custom-650x300-Design-Milk-2020.gif":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx6/cdn100@2020_1/2020/09/16/05-03-44-526_4b374a3338454e2d.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~r/design-milk/~4/x_X2eHgzSDU":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx3/cdn74@2020_5/2020/09/16/05-03-43-042_43469e171ab9d841.webp"},"publishedOrCreatedDate":1600232607171},{"createdTime":"2020-09-16 13:03:27","updatedTime":"2020-09-16 13:03:27","title":"LG PuriCare Wearable Air Purifier Makes Breathing a Little Easier","link":"https://design-milk.com/?p=427317","description":"<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/lg-puricare-wearable-air-purifier/lg-puricare-wearable-air-purifier-lifestyle/\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/08/LG-PuriCare-Wearable-Air-Purifier-LIFESTYLE-810x463.jpg\" alt=\"LG PuriCare Wearable Air Purifier Makes Breathing a Little Easier\" /></a></p> \n<p>Wearing a mask in public is a civic-minded act that helps protect the most vulnerable from infection. But wearing a mask can become both uncomfortable and ineffective if improperly fit and/or when the filtering material impedes breathing. The <a href=\"https://www.lg.com/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer external\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">LG</a> PuriCare Wearable Air Purifier announced at <a href=\"https://www.lg.com/global/exhibition/main.jsp\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer external\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">IFA 2020</a> addresses both issues with an auto-powered air purification solution.</p> \n<div id=\"attachment_427319\" class=\"wp-caption alignnone\">\n <a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=427319\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-427319\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"wp-image-427319 size-full\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/08/LG-PuriCare-Wearable-Air-Purifier-01-1.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"540\" height=\"405\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/08/LG-PuriCare-Wearable-Air-Purifier-01-1.jpg 540w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/08/LG-PuriCare-Wearable-Air-Purifier-01-1-500x375.jpg 500w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 540px) 100vw, 540px\" /></a>\n <p class=\"wp-caption-text\">The PuriCare Wearable Air Purifier is fitted with two H13 HEPA filters, similar to the filters used in the company’s home air purifier products. LG has yet to certify whether the mask’s filtration operates while exhaling as it does with every inhale.</p>\n</div> \n<p>The PuriCare Wearable is in essence a miniaturized and wearable air purifier. Equipped with a Respiratory Sensor, the mask’s filtration system kicks in automatically in response to the wearer’s breathing using dual three-speed fans; the two fans automatically speed up to assist air intake and slow down to reduce resistance when exhaling. In theory, this filtration alongside the ergonomic face-hugging design should make wearing a mask a noticeably more comfortable affair while also improving the efficacy of filtration.</p> \n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=427320\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-427320\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"alignnone wp-image-427320\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/08/LG-PuriCare-Wearable-Air-Purifier-02-1.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"608\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/08/LG-PuriCare-Wearable-Air-Purifier-02-1.jpg 540w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/08/LG-PuriCare-Wearable-Air-Purifier-02-1-500x375.jpg 500w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p> \n<p>The mask is powered by a lightweight 820mAh battery offering up to eight hours of operation in low flow mode, but this rating drops down to just two hours when set to its maximum fan setting.</p> \n<div id=\"attachment_427321\" class=\"wp-caption alignnone\">\n <a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=427321\" rel=\"attachment and ear straps are both replaceable and recyclable, but pricing for the mask and its accessories is currently unavailable.</p>\n</div> \n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=427322\" charging case equipped with integrated UV-LED lights engineered to destroy harmful germs between uses. The case can be tethered to the LG ThinQ mobile app to send notifications when the filters need to be replaced.</p> \n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/?attachment_id=427323\" rel=\"attachment 13:03:27","updatedTime":"2020-09-16 13:03:27","title":"From Chaos To Calm: Moisés Hernandez","link":"https://design-milk.com/?p=428557","description":"<p><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">The following post is brought to you by </span></i><a href=\"https://ad.doubleclick.net/ddm/trackclk/N718679.1204842DESIGN-MILK.COM/B23668231.281869426;dc_trk_aid=475781413;dc_trk_cid=137507113;dc_lat=;dc_rdid=;tag_for_child_directed_treatment=;tfua=;gdpr=${GDPR};gdpr_consent=${GDPR_CONSENT_755}\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored external noreferrer\" data-wpel-link=\"external\"><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">Squarespace</span></i></a><i><span style=\"font-weight: 400;\">, an easy-to-use website builder for your personal and professional needs. You can start a free trial for a website (with no credit card required) today and use coupon code DESIGNMILK for 10% off your website when you’re ready to publish. Our partners are hand picked by the Design Milk team because they represent the best in design.</span></i></p> \n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/from-chaos-to-calm-moises-hernandez/moises-profile-squarespace/\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Moises-Profile-squarespace-810x540.jpeg\" alt=\"From Chaos To Calm: Moisés Hernandez\" /></a></p> \n<p>Rising above a tree-shaded avenue perpendicular to Mexico City’s cultural center, Bosque de Chapultepec, behind a monochromatic facade pockmarked with porthole windows, <a href=\"http://www.moises-hernandez.com/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer external\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">Studio Moisés Hernández</a> operates as a placid promontory for a team of young designers led by its founder and studio namesake, Moisés Hernandez. Working diligently together since 2014, the team has helped establish Mexico City as one of the most exciting and compelling design capitals in the world today.</p> \n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/from-chaos-to-calm-moises-hernandez/moises_hernandez_squarespace-diario-2/\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-428559\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-428559\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Moises_Hernandez_squarespace-Diario-2-810x418.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"418\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Moises_Hernandez_squarespace-Diario-2-810x418.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Moises_Hernandez_squarespace-Diario-2-800x413.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Moises_Hernandez_squarespace-Diario-2-768x397.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Moises_Hernandez_squarespace-Diario-2-500x258.jpg 500w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Moises_Hernandez_squarespace-Diario-2.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p> \n<p>Crafted yet modern, identifiably regional yet appeasingly global –– Moisés Hernandez’s designs explore the razor’s edge between the contradictory and cohesive, with his city prominently the muse to his maker. “<em>Mexico City is chaotic</em>,” says Hernandez, “<em>Especially in the center area where my studio and home are located… it is a very creative place with a wide range of disciplines, such as contemporary art, music and design. Moreover, it is an area full of improvised expressions and eclectic architecture; in the same street you can see modern buildings, classical architecture and self-built houses, which are very unique and represent the idea of creating something based on your instincts and personal tastes.</em>”</p> \n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/from-chaos-to-calm-moises-hernandez/moises-profile-squarespace-2/\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-428560\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-428560\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Moises-Profile-squarespace-2-810x540.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"540\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Moises-Profile-squarespace-2-810x540.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Moises-Profile-squarespace-2-800x534.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Moises-Profile-squarespace-2-768x512.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Moises-Profile-squarespace-2-500x334.jpg 500w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Moises-Profile-squarespace-2.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p> \n<p>As the first Mexican to graduate from Ecal, Ecole Cantonale d’Art de Lausanne in the Master Product Design program in Switzerland in 2013, Hernandez would return to Mexico City to open his own studio. With a refreshed perspective, the young designer immediately began recontextualizing the deep seeded traditions, textures and chromatic expressions unique not only to Mexico City, but numerous surrounding regions characterized by their own distinct arts and crafts, then applying them to projects as diverse as <a href=\"http://www.moises-hernandez.com/eclipse\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer external\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">jewelry</a>, <a href=\"http://www.moises-hernandez.com/land\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer external\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">bathroom hardware</a> and <a href=\"http://www.moises-hernandez.com/materia\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer external\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">furniture</a>.</p> \n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/from-chaos-to-calm-moises-hernandez/moises_hernandez_squarespace-waterfaucet-moises/\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-428561\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-428561\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Moises_Hernandez_squarespace-WaterFaucet-Moises-810x539.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"539\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Moises_Hernandez_squarespace-WaterFaucet-Moises-810x539.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Moises_Hernandez_squarespace-WaterFaucet-Moises-800x533.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Moises_Hernandez_squarespace-WaterFaucet-Moises-768x511.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Moises_Hernandez_squarespace-WaterFaucet-Moises-500x333.jpg 500w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Moises_Hernandez_squarespace-WaterFaucet-Moises.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p> \n<p>“<em>I came back from Switzerland with the idea to create everyday Mexican objects and aesthetic solutions for national and international clients based on two principles — efficiency and perfection — but always considering my own context.</em>”</p> \n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/from-chaos-to-calm-moises-hernandez/moises_hernandez_squarespace-moiseshernandez-website2/\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-428562\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-428562\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Moises_Hernandez_squarespace-MoisesHernandez-website2-810x532.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"532\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Moises_Hernandez_squarespace-MoisesHernandez-website2-810x532.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Moises_Hernandez_squarespace-MoisesHernandez-website2-800x525.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Moises_Hernandez_squarespace-MoisesHernandez-website2-768x504.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Moises_Hernandez_squarespace-MoisesHernandez-website2-500x328.jpg 500w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Moises_Hernandez_squarespace-MoisesHernandez-website2.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p> \n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/from-chaos-to-calm-moises-hernandez/moises_hernandez_squarespace-moiseshernandez-website3/\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-428563\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-428563\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Moises_Hernandez_squarespace-MoisesHernandez-website3-810x606.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"606\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Moises_Hernandez_squarespace-MoisesHernandez-website3-810x606.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Moises_Hernandez_squarespace-MoisesHernandez-website3-800x598.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Moises_Hernandez_squarespace-MoisesHernandez-website3-768x574.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Moises_Hernandez_squarespace-MoisesHernandez-website3-500x374.jpg 500w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Moises_Hernandez_squarespace-MoisesHernandez-website3.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p> \n<p>Alongside his studio, Hernandez would immediately create a website to complement the launch; the site has evolved over the years and now sits on <a href=\"https://ad.doubleclick.net/ddm/trackclk/N718679.1204842DESIGN-MILK.COM/B23668231.281869426;dc_trk_aid=475781413;dc_trk_cid=137507113;dc_lat=;dc_rdid=;tag_for_child_directed_treatment=;tfua=;gdpr=${GDPR};gdpr_consent=${GDPR_CONSENT_755}\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored noreferrer external\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">Squarespace</a>. “<em>I opened my first website ten years ago when I was 26 years old, and I remember only a few designers my age had one then</em>,” recollects Hernandez, “<em>Today, I think having a website is a must for every designer or creative person. It is a tool that helps you to show your work as a business card, and you have more chances to be reached from different people, clients and companies.</em>”</p> \n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/from-chaos-to-calm-moises-hernandez/moises_hernandez_squarespace-moiseshernandez-website/\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-428565\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-428565\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Moises_Hernandez_squarespace-MoisesHernandez-website-810x608.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"608\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Moises_Hernandez_squarespace-MoisesHernandez-website-810x608.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Moises_Hernandez_squarespace-MoisesHernandez-website-800x600.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Moises_Hernandez_squarespace-MoisesHernandez-website-768x576.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Moises_Hernandez_squarespace-MoisesHernandez-website-500x375.jpg 500w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Moises_Hernandez_squarespace-MoisesHernandez-website.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p> \n<p>While chaos may reign supreme outside his studio doors, Hernandez’s work is observably serene, a trait identifiable in his most recent work for French modern furniture company, Lignet Roset. With subtle references to Mexican folk art, the double-sided <a href=\"http://www.moises-hernandez.com/mascara\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer external\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">Máscara throw blanket</a> is executed with a precise patterning softened by a woven warmth; the result would look equally natural wrapped around your abuela as draped across a perfectly staged sofa in Silver Lake.</p> \n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/from-chaos-to-calm-moises-hernandez/no_vase_moises-hernandez/\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-428567\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-428567\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/No_Vase_Moises-Hernandez-810x530.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"530\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/No_Vase_Moises-Hernandez-810x530.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/No_Vase_Moises-Hernandez-800x524.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/No_Vase_Moises-Hernandez-768x503.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/No_Vase_Moises-Hernandez-500x327.jpg 500w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/No_Vase_Moises-Hernandez.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p> \n<p>Similarly, <a href=\"http://www.moises-hernandez.com/no-vase\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer external\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">No vase</a>, a reductive amalgamation of stainless steel, brass and copper designed to display flora with serene singularity offers a Mexican counterpart to the Japanese concept of Ma (間),the observation and utilization of negative space.</p> \n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/from-chaos-to-calm-moises-hernandez/no_vase_moises-hernandez-2/\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-428568\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-428568\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/No_Vase_Moises-Hernandez-2-810x538.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"538\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/No_Vase_Moises-Hernandez-2-810x538.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/No_Vase_Moises-Hernandez-2-800x531.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/No_Vase_Moises-Hernandez-2-768x510.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/No_Vase_Moises-Hernandez-2-500x332.jpg 500w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/No_Vase_Moises-Hernandez-2.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p> \n<blockquote>\n <p>This chaotic environment in Mexico City forces me to seek the opposite: slower and quieter. Oaxaca is very similar to Kyoto, Japan.</p>\n</blockquote> \n<p>While a passion for the vernacular tradition plays prominent, Hernandez notes a disinterest in over-romanticizing traditional craft. Instead, Hernandez relies upon technology to enhance traditional craft, a “whimsical dichotomy” of past and present.</p> \n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/from-chaos-to-calm-moises-hernandez/moises_hernandez_squarespace-pujol_moiseshernandez-1/\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-428569\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-428569\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Moises_Hernandez_squarespace-Pujol_MoisesHernandez-1-810x541.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"541\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Moises_Hernandez_squarespace-Pujol_MoisesHernandez-1-810x541.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Moises_Hernandez_squarespace-Pujol_MoisesHernandez-1-800x534.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Moises_Hernandez_squarespace-Pujol_MoisesHernandez-1-768x513.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Moises_Hernandez_squarespace-Pujol_MoisesHernandez-1-500x334.jpg 500w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Moises_Hernandez_squarespace-Pujol_MoisesHernandez-1.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p> \n<p><em>“The dishware we designed for Enrique Olvera’s restaurant <a href=\"https://pujol.com.mx/en/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer external\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">Pujol</a> was based upon the <a href=\"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Talavera_pottery\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer external\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">traditional Mexican talavera</a>. We cut the jigs with a laser cutter, then the artisans used them to neatly and efficiently create all 42 ceramic forms. I think Mexican designers should be able to understand and master the possibilities that both worlds give you in order to make clever decisions.”</em></p> \n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/from-chaos-to-calm-moises-hernandez/moises_hernandez_squarespace-pujol_moiseshernandez-2/\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-428570\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-428570\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Moises_Hernandez_squarespace-Pujol_MoisesHernandez-2-810x537.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"537\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Moises_Hernandez_squarespace-Pujol_MoisesHernandez-2-810x537.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Moises_Hernandez_squarespace-Pujol_MoisesHernandez-2.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p> \n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/from-chaos-to-calm-moises-hernandez/moises_hernandez_squarespace-pujol_moiseshernandez-3/\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-428571\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-428571\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Moises_Hernandez_squarespace-Pujol_MoisesHernandez-3-810x537.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"537\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Moises_Hernandez_squarespace-Pujol_MoisesHernandez-3-810x537.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Moises_Hernandez_squarespace-Pujol_MoisesHernandez-3-800x530.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Moises_Hernandez_squarespace-Pujol_MoisesHernandez-3-768x509.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Moises_Hernandez_squarespace-Pujol_MoisesHernandez-3-500x331.jpg 500w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Moises_Hernandez_squarespace-Pujol_MoisesHernandez-3.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p> \n<p>Hernandez’s secret weapon and key collaborator is Mexico City’s vibrant population of skilled woodworkers, metalsmiths and glassblowers. <em>“These workshops represent an opportunity where both parts, designers and makers, and the result can be very fruitful… establishing authentic relationships based upon trust and honesty.”</em></p> \n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/from-chaos-to-calm-moises-hernandez/moises_hernandez_squarespace-diario-themap/\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-428572\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-428572\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Moises_Hernandez_squarespace-Diario-TheMap-810x697.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"697\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Moises_Hernandez_squarespace-Diario-TheMap-810x697.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Moises_Hernandez_squarespace-Diario-TheMap-800x688.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Moises_Hernandez_squarespace-Diario-TheMap-768x661.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Moises_Hernandez_squarespace-Diario-TheMap-500x430.jpg 500w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Moises_Hernandez_squarespace-Diario-TheMap.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p> \n<p>The reality of COVID-19 has dampened some of <a href=\"http://www.moises-hernandez.com/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer external\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">Studio Moisés Hernández’s</a> planned projects for 2020, but Hernandez is enthused to point out visitors can check out <a href=\"http://www.diarioshop.com/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer external\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">Diario</a> (Spanish for <em>diary</em>), one of the designer’s side projects which he built on <a href=\"https://ad.doubleclick.net/ddm/trackclk/N718679.1204842DESIGN-MILK.COM/B23668231.281869426;dc_trk_aid=475781413;dc_trk_cid=137507113;dc_lat=;dc_rdid=;tag_for_child_directed_treatment=;tfua=;gdpr=${GDPR};gdpr_consent=${GDPR_CONSENT_755}\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noopener sponsored noreferrer external\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">Squarespace</a> and used to transcribe seven years of personal notes into an online journal documenting craftspeople and their techniques discovered while traveling across numerous parts of Mexico.</p> \n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/from-chaos-to-calm-moises-hernandez/moises_hernandez_squarespace-diario_mapa/\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-428573\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-428573\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Moises_Hernandez_squarespace-Diario_mapa-810x537.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"537\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Moises_Hernandez_squarespace-Diario_mapa-810x537.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Moises_Hernandez_squarespace-Diario_mapa-800x530.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Moises_Hernandez_squarespace-Diario_mapa-768x509.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Moises_Hernandez_squarespace-Diario_mapa-500x331.jpg 500w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Moises_Hernandez_squarespace-Diario_mapa.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p> \n<p><em>Some of the [Diario] projects enhance the beauty of the traditional crafts, like the textiles that we created in collaboration with Felipe in Oaxaca or the Palm Woven, a tribute to palm where we collaborated with women from Tlamacazapa, Guerrero. While some others are a contemporary version of some everyday objects made by local makers in Mexico City – the Mercado Bag, Mexico Map or the glass tumblers.”</em></p> \n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/from-chaos-to-calm-moises-hernandez/moises_hernandez_squarespace-dsc_0268copy/\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-428574\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-428574\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Moises_Hernandez_squarespace-DSC_0268copy-810x537.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"537\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Moises_Hernandez_squarespace-DSC_0268copy-810x537.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Moises_Hernandez_squarespace-DSC_0268copy-800x530.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Moises_Hernandez_squarespace-DSC_0268copy-768x509.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Moises_Hernandez_squarespace-DSC_0268copy-500x331.jpg 500w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Moises_Hernandez_squarespace-DSC_0268copy.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p> \n<p><a href=\"https://design-milk.com/from-chaos-to-calm-moises-hernandez/moises_hernandez_squarespace-dsc_0206/\" rel=\"attachment wp-att-428575\" data-wpel-link=\"internal\"><img class=\"alignnone size-large wp-image-428575\" src=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Moises_Hernandez_squarespace-DSC_0206-810x537.jpg\" alt=\"\" width=\"810\" height=\"537\" srcset=\"https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Moises_Hernandez_squarespace-DSC_0206-810x537.jpg 810w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Moises_Hernandez_squarespace-DSC_0206-800x530.jpg 800w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Moises_Hernandez_squarespace-DSC_0206-768x509.jpg 768w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Moises_Hernandez_squarespace-DSC_0206-500x331.jpg 500w, https://design-milk.com/images/2020/09/Moises_Hernandez_squarespace-DSC_0206.jpg 1280w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 810px) 100vw, 810px\" /></a></p> \n<p>Additionally, 2020 still offers a forthcoming collaboration with Mexican manufacturer, <a href=\"https://mexadesign.com/en/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer external\" data-wpel-link=\"external\">Mexa</a> translating vernacular seating forms into a contemporary form, alongside mention of a more mysterious project for 2021 <em>“based on color and its different possibilities”</em> informed by&nbsp;<em>“massive research about materials, techniques and pigments.”</em></p> \n<p>Despite all of the trials and tribulations of operating in the midst of a global pandemic today, Hernandez harbors high hopes looking forward. <em>“The future of the Mexican design scene seems very exciting and positive. Young designers, skilled crafts people and creatives coming from all over the world now form Mexico City’s creative community, and events like our own Design Week Mexico, alongside Abierto Mexicano de Diseño and Zona Maco Diseño celebrate it.”</em></p> \n<p><em>Ready to share your vision or brand with the world?
